Similarly to the book, we can introduce equational reasoning in agda.
I'm using the definitions from the [agda-stdlib](https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2708).

## 2.7 Σ-types

I'm using a slightly different definition of the `f` in the following
theorem, as it'll be useful further on.

## 2.8 The unit type

<pre class="Agda"><a id="13311" class="Comment">-- Theorem 2.8.1.</a>
<a id="≡-𝟙-≃"></a><a id="13329" href="Chapter2.Book.html#13329" class="Function">≡-𝟙-≃</a> <a id="13335" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13337" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13338" href="Chapter2.Book.html#13338" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13340" href="Chapter2.Book.html#13340" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="13342" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13344" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1315" class="Datatype">𝟙</a><a id="13345" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13347" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13349" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13350" href="Chapter2.Book.html#13338" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13352" href="Chapter1.Book.html#3989" class="Function Operator">≡</a> <a id="13354" href="Chapter2.Book.html#13340" class="Bound">y</a><a id="13355" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13357" href="Chapter2.Book.html#7900" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="13359" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1315" class="Datatype">𝟙</a>
<a id="13361" href="Chapter2.Book.html#13329" class="Function">≡-𝟙-≃</a> <a id="13367" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1330" class="InductiveConstructor">⋆</a> <a id="13369" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1330" class="InductiveConstructor">⋆</a> <a id="13371" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13373" href="Chapter2.Book.html#13415" class="Function">f</a> <a id="13375" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1517" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13377" href="Chapter2.Book.html#7412" class="Function">invs⇒equivs</a> <a id="13389" href="Chapter2.Book.html#13415" class="Function">f</a> <a id="13391" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13392" href="Chapter2.Book.html#13445" class="Function">g</a> <a id="13394" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1517" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13396" href="Chapter2.Book.html#13480" class="Function">α</a> <a id="13398" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1517" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13400" href="Chapter2.Book.html#13527" class="Function">β</a><a id="13401" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="13405" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="13415" href="Chapter2.Book.html#13415" class="Function">f</a> <a id="13417" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13419" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1330" class="InductiveConstructor">⋆</a> <a id="13421" href="Chapter1.Book.html#3989" class="Function Operator">≡</a> <a id="13423" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1330" class="InductiveConstructor">⋆</a> <a id="13425" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13427" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1315" class="Datatype">𝟙</a>
    <a id="13433" href="Chapter2.Book.html#13415" class="Function">f</a> <a id="13435" href="Chapter2.Book.html#13435" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="13437" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13439" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1330" class="InductiveConstructor">⋆</a>
    <a id="13445" href="Chapter2.Book.html#13445" class="Function">g</a> <a id="13447" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13449" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1315" class="Datatype">𝟙</a> <a id="13451" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13453" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1330" class="InductiveConstructor">⋆</a> <a id="13455" href="Chapter1.Book.html#3989" class="Function Operator">≡</a> <a id="13457" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1330" class="InductiveConstructor">⋆</a>
    <a id="13463" href="Chapter2.Book.html#13445" class="Function">g</a> <a id="13465" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1330" class="InductiveConstructor">⋆</a> <a id="13467" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13469" href="Chapter1.Book.html#3949" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="13474" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1330" class="InductiveConstructor">⋆</a>

## 2.10 Universes and the univalence axiom

<pre class="Agda"><a id="15224" class="Comment">-- Lemma 2.10.1.</a>
<a id="idtoeqv"></a><a id="15241" href="Chapter2.Book.html#15241" class="Function">idtoeqv</a> <a id="15249" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15251" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15252" href="Chapter2.Book.html#15252" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="15254" href="Chapter2.Book.html#15254" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="15256" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15258" href="Chapter1.Book.html#343" class="Function">𝒰</a> <a id="15260" href="Chapter1.Book.html#328" class="Generalizable">𝒾</a><a id="15261" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15263" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15265" href="Chapter2.Book.html#15252" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="15267" href="Chapter1.Book.html#3989" class="Function Operator">≡</a> <a id="15269" href="Chapter2.Book.html#15254" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="15271" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15273" href="Chapter2.Book.html#15252" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="15275" href="Chapter2.Book.html#7900" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="15277" href="Chapter2.Book.html#15254" class="Bound">B</a>
<a id="15279" href="Chapter2.Book.html#15241" class="Function">idtoeqv</a> <a id="15287" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15288" href="Chapter2.Book.html#15288" class="Bound">𝒾</a><a id="15289" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15291" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15292" href="Chapter2.Book.html#15292" class="Bound">A</a><a id="15293" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15295" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15296" href="Chapter2.Book.html#15296" class="Bound">B</a><a id="15297" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15299" href="Chapter2.Book.html#15299" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="15301" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15303" href="Chapter2.Book.html#4324" class="Function">tr</a> <a id="15306" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="15309" href="Chapter2.Book.html#15309" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="15311" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15313" href="Chapter2.Book.html#15309" class="Bound">C</a><a id="15314" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15316" href="Chapter2.Book.html#15299" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="15318" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1517" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="15320" href="Chapter2.Book.html#15341" class="Function">helper</a> <a id="15327" href="Chapter2.Book.html#15299" class="Bound">p</a>

## 2.11 Identity type

<pre class="Agda"><a id="20001" class="Comment">-- Lemma 2.11.2.</a>
<a id="isEquiv⇒isEquiv-ap"></a><a id="20018" href="Chapter2.Book.html#20018" class="Function">isEquiv⇒isEquiv-ap</a> <a id="20037" class="Symbol">:</a>
             <a id="20052" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20053" href="Chapter2.Book.html#20053" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="20055" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20057" href="Chapter1.Book.html#343" class="Function">𝒰</a> <a id="20059" href="Chapter1.Book.html#328" class="Generalizable">𝒾</a><a id="20060" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="20062" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="20063" href="Chapter2.Book.html#20063" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="20065" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20067" href="Chapter1.Book.html#343" class="Function">𝒰</a> <a id="20069" href="Chapter1.Book.html#328" class="Generalizable">𝒾</a><a id="20070" class="Symbol">}</a>
           <a id="20083" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20085" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="20086" href="Chapter2.Book.html#20086" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="20088" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="20090" href="Chapter2.Book.html#20053" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="20092" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20094" href="Chapter2.Book.html#20063" class="Bound">B</a><a id="20095" class="Symbol">)</a>
           <a id="20108" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="20110" href="Chapter2.Book.html#7240" class="Function">isEquiv</a> <a id="20118" href="Chapter2.Book.html#20086" class="Bound">f</a>
